      <div class="sqs-layout sqs-grid-12 columns-12" data-type="page-section" id="page-section-61436de52e743e18f1d6c27b"><div class="row sqs-row"><div class="col sqs-col-12 span-12"><div class="sqs-block code-block sqs-block-code" data-block-type="23" id="block-yui_3_17_2_1_1593029317331_67976"><div class="sqs-block-content"><p id="privacy-summary" class="preFade" style="transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.0649682s;"></p></div></div><div class="sqs-block html-block sqs-block-html" data-block-type="2" id="block-5ef38e226c86a07a9fc23a97"><div class="sqs-block-content">

<div class="sqs-html-content">
  <h3 style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.066879s;" class="preSlide">SUMMARY</h3><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.0687898s;">The following is a short summary of the key elements of this Privacy Policy, but please review our full privacy policy, below, before using the site.</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.0707006s;">We may collect personal information from or about you, including personal contact information, demographic information, payment information, and user content you submit to us.&nbsp;</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.0726115s;">We primarily use this information in connection with your relationship with MWM, your use of the Services, processing your transactions, improving our Services, for sending you information from us, and tailoring the information we provide to you. We also automatically collect information through your use of the Services, which may include information about your location inferred from your IP address, as well as usage information about your device, such as&nbsp; browser and operating system, how you arrived at our Services, device identifiers, and information received through our use of cookies and other technologies. We may also collect information about you from third parties. Please review the “INFORMATION WE MAY COLLECT THROUGH THE SERVICES” and “HOW WE MAY USE THE INFORMATION COLLECTED” sections of this Privacy Policy for a full description of the information we collect and how we use that information.</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.0745223s;">We may share your information with third parties, for example, third party service providers, in relation to sweepstakes, contests, and promotions, and for administrative and legal reasons. For full details, please review the section below titled “HOW WE MAY USE THE INFORMATION COLLECTED”.</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.0764331s;">We also offer you choices on what we do with your information, and offer those who have an online account&nbsp; the opportunity to view, update, or edit account registration data. For more detail, please see the section titled “ACCESSING AND UPDATING YOUR INFORMATION AND YOUR CHOICES”. If you are a California resident, please see the “<a href="#ca-resident-notice">NOTICE TO CALIFORNIA RESIDENTS</a>” section for more information about your rights; or if you are a Nevada resident please see the <a href="#nv-resident-notice">NOTICE TO NEVADA RESIDENTS</a>" section for more information about your rights.</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.0783439s;">We employ commercially reasonable administrative, technical and physical safeguards; however, no system can be guaranteed 100% secure. We therefore cannot ensure or warrant the security of any information that you transmit to us, or that we transmit to you</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.0802548s;">How to contact us: For more information about this Privacy Policy and our privacy practices, please contact <a href="mailto:legal@madisonwellsmedia.com">legal@madisonwellsmedia.com</a>.</p>
</div>



</div></div><div class="sqs-block code-block sqs-block-code" data-block-type="23" id="block-yui_3_17_2_1_1593029317331_100722"><div class="sqs-block-content"><p id="info-collected-servers" class="preFade" style="transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.0821656s;"><a id="back-to-top" href="#top">Back to Top ⇡</a></p></div></div><div class="sqs-block html-block sqs-block-html" data-block-type="2" id="block-yui_3_17_2_1_1593029317331_100788"><div class="sqs-block-content">

<div class="sqs-html-content">
  <h3 style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.0840764s;" class="preSlide">INFORMATION WE MAY COLLECT THROUGH THE SERVICES</h3><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.0859873s;">We collect information from you directly, automatically when you visit the Services, and sometimes from third parties. Some of this information may be considered “personal information” under various applicable laws. We consider information that identifies you as a specific, identified individual to be personal information (such as contact information), and we treat additional information, including IP addresses and cookie identifiers, as “personal information” where required by applicable law. And, if we combine information we consider to be non-personal with personal information, we will treat that combined information as personal information under this Privacy Policy and as required by law. Note that we may de-identify personal information so that it is non-personal, such as aggregating or converting it to a code, sometimes using a function commonly known as a “hash”. We will treat de-identified information as non-personal to the fullest extent allowed by applicable law.</p>
</div>



</div></div><div class="sqs-block code-block sqs-block-code" data-block-type="23" id="block-yui_3_17_2_1_1593029317331_123712"><div class="sqs-block-content"><p id="info-provided" class="preFade" style="transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.0878981s;"><a id="back-to-top" href="#top">Back to Top ⇡</a></p></div></div><div class="sqs-block html-block sqs-block-html" data-block-type="2" id="block-yui_3_17_2_1_1593029317331_123778"><div class="sqs-block-content">

<div class="sqs-html-content">
  <h3 style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.0898089s;" class="preSlide">Information You Provide to Us Directly&nbsp;</h3><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.0917197s;">MWM may ask you to provide information directly when you interact with us, such as contact information, including your name, phone number, mailing address, and email address, other information about you, such as demographic information (ZIP code, gender, and day and month of birth, for example) and information about your interests and preferences. <div class="sqs-html-content">
  <h3 style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.0974522s;" class="preSlide">Information We Collect Automatically As You Access the Services&nbsp;</h3><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.0993631s;">We, and our third-party business partners (including any third-party service providers or third party advertising, content, or analytics providers), may use a variety of technologies that automatically or passively collect certain information about your use of the Services whenever you visit or interact with the Services (<strong>“Usage Information”</strong>). This Usage Information may include the website browser or operating system you are using, the URL that referred you to our Services, the search terms you entered into a search engine that led you to our Services, all of the areas within our Services that you visit, and the time of day, the next website you visit after leaving our Services, among other information. We may use this Usage Information for a variety of purposes, including analyzing trends, administering the Services, tracking users' movements around the Services, gathering demographic information about our user base as a whole, and enhancing or otherwise improving the Services. As you use the Services, we may also track videos you watch and audio you listen to and how you interact with the content. You acknowledge that, if you choose to post any information about your video watching or viewing history on a third-party platform or in the MWM Community (described below), the Video Privacy Protection Act of 1998 (18 U.S.C. § 2710) (or any similar state law) does not apply. However, to the extent it does apply in any manner, you are providing your informed, written consent to the disclosure of that information pursuant to the Video Privacy Protection Act.&nbsp;</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.101274s;">In addition, we automatically collect your IP address or other unique identifier (<strong>“Device Identifier”</strong>) for your computer, mobile phone, or other device used to access the Services. A Device Identifier is a number that is automatically assigned to your device used to access the Services, and our servers identify your device by its Device Identifier. We may be able to collect or infer your approximate location based on your Device Identifier or similar information we collect.&nbsp;</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.103185s;">We use the following types of tracking technologies to automatically collect information when you interact with us online:&nbsp;</p>
</div>



</div></div><div class="sqs-block code-block sqs-block-code" data-block-type="23" id="block-yui_3_17_2_1_1593029317331_151381"><div class="sqs-block-content"><p id="cookies-local-storage" class="preFade" style="transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.105096s;"></p></div></div><div class="sqs-block html-block sqs-block-html" data-block-type="2" id="block-yui_3_17_2_1_1593029317331_151447"><div class="sqs-block-content">

<div class="sqs-html-content">
  <p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.107006s;">Cookies and Local Storage. “Cookies” and local storage are pieces of information (data files) transferred to an individual’s browser on their device when the device is used to visit a Site. These technologies are able to store a unique identifier for a device to allow a certain Internet site to recognize the device whenever the device is used to visit the Services. These technologies may be used for many purposes by us and our third-party service providers, such as automatically collecting Usage Information, enabling features, and remembering your preferences. We may use cookies and other technologies to study traffic patterns on our Services, to make them even more rewarding as well as to study the effectiveness of our customer communications. And we may use cookies to customize your experience and provide greater convenience each time you interact with us. The information we store includes internet protocol (IP) addresses, browser type, Internet service provider (ISP), referring/exit pages, operating system, date/time stamp, and clickstream data. If you do not want to accept cookies, you can block them by adjusting the settings on your Internet browser. You can find more information about cookies and how they work at <a href="http://allaboutcookies.org" target="_blank">allaboutcookies.org</a>.</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.108917s;">If you choose to disable cookies or restrict local storage, some features of the Services may not function properly.&nbsp;</p>
</div>



</div></div><div class="sqs-block code-block sqs-block-code" data-block-type="23" id="block-yui_3_17_2_1_1593029317331_154506"><div class="sqs-block-content"><p id="pixel-tags" class="preFade" style="transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.110828s;"></p></div></div><div class="sqs-block html-block sqs-block-html" data-block-type="2" id="block-yui_3_17_2_1_1593029317331_154572"><div class="sqs-block-content">

<div class="sqs-html-content">
  <p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.112739s;">Pixel tags. Pixel tags are tiny graphic images or other web programming code that tell us what parts of our website customers have visited or to measure the effectiveness of searches customers perform on our Services. Pixel tags and similar technologies may be used for a number of purposes, including, without limitation, to count visitors to a Site, to monitor how users navigate the Services, to count how many emails that were sent were actually opened, to count how many particular links were actually viewed. Pixel tags also enable us to send e-mail messages in a format customers can read.&nbsp;</p>
</div>



</div></div><div class="sqs-block code-block sqs-block-code" data-block-type="23" id="block-yui_3_17_2_1_1593029317331_182093"><div class="sqs-block-content"><p id="embed-scripts" class="preFade" style="transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.11465s;"></p></div></div><div class="sqs-block html-block sqs-block-html" data-block-type="2" id="block-yui_3_17_2_1_1593029317331_182159"><div class="sqs-block-content">

<div class="sqs-html-content">
  <p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.116561s;">Embedded Scripts. An embedded script is programming code that is designed to collect information about your interactions with the Services, such as the links you click on. The code is temporarily downloaded onto your device from our server or a third-party service provider, is active only while you are connected to a Site, and is deactivated or deleted thereafter.</p>
</div>



</div></div><div class="sqs-block code-block sqs-block-code" data-block-type="23" id="block-yui_3_17_2_1_1593029317331_184948"><div class="sqs-block-content"><p id="click-thru-urls" class="preFade" style="transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.118471s;"></p></div></div><div class="sqs-block html-block sqs-block-html" data-block-type="2" id="block-yui_3_17_2_1_1593029317331_185014"><div class="sqs-block-content">

<div class="sqs-html-content">
  <p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.120382s;">Click Through URLs.<strong> </strong>In some of our e-mail messages we use a "click-through URL" linked to content on the Services. When a customer clicks one of these URLs, they pass through our web server before arriving at the destination web page. We track this click-through data to help us determine interest in particular topics and measure the effectiveness of our customer communications.&nbsp;</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.122293s;">In addition, we may use a variety of other technologies that collect similar information for security and fraud detection<strong> </strong>purposes.</p>

</div></div><div class="sqs-block spacer-block sqs-block-spacer sized vsize-1" data-block-type="21" id="block-yui_3_17_2_1_1593027892759_76182"><div class="sqs-block-content">&nbsp;</div></div><div class="sqs-block html-block sqs-block-html" data-block-type="2" id="block-yui_3_17_2_1_1593027892759_76630"><div class="sqs-block-content">

<div class="sqs-html-content">
  <h3 style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.489172s;" class="preSlide">Inferences drawn from any of the information identified above to create a profile about a consumer</h3><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.491083s;"><em>These inferences may relate to your perceived interests, preferences, characteristics, or behavior.</em>&nbsp;</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.492994s;"><strong>We may collect this type of information from:</strong></p><ul data-rte-list="default"><li><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.494904s;">Consumers;</p></li><li><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.496815s;">Cookies and tracking technologies;</p></li><li><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.498726s;">Third party social media companies;</p></li><li><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.500637s;">Third party business partners and service providers, such as data analytics providers.</p></li></ul><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.502548s;"><strong>We may use this type of information to:</strong></p><ul data-rte-list="default"><li><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.504459s;">Personalize your experience and tailor content we display to you, such as advertising, recommendations, promotions, and offers we display to you;&nbsp;</p></li><li><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.506369s;">Further internal business purposes, such as to improve our Services or our products and services, and to comply with regulatory and legal obligations;&nbsp;</p></li><li><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.50828s;">As disclosed at the time you provide your information or otherwise with your consent.</p></li></ul><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; </div></div><div class="sqs-block code-block sqs-block-code" data-block-type="23" id="block-yui_3_17_2_1_1593051080584_37547"><div class="sqs-block-content"><p id="ca-deletion-rights" class="preFade" style="transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.523567s;"><a id="back-to-top" href="#top">Back to Top ⇡</a></p></div></div><div class="sqs-block html-block sqs-block-html" data-block-type="2" id="block-yui_3_17_2_1_1593023812016_55737"><div class="sqs-block-content">

<div class="sqs-html-content">
  <h3 style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.525478s;" class="preSlide">EXERCISING YOUR CALIFORNIA ACCESS AND DELETION RIGHTS&nbsp;</h3><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.527389s;">California residents have the right to request: (1) that we disclose to you what Personal Information we collect, use, disclose, and sell, including the right to request that we provide to you the specific pieces of Personal Information we have collected about you in the prior 12 months (“Right to Know”); and (2) that we delete the Personal Information we collect about you (“Right to Delete”), all subject to exceptions set forth in the CCPA.&nbsp; More information on these rights is below.&nbsp;</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.529299s;"><strong>Agents</strong></p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.53121s;">If you are an agent submitting a request on a user’s behalf, please send an email to <a href="mailto:legal@madisonwellsmedia.com">legal@madisonwellsmedia.com</a> with a declaration signed by the individual who is the subject of the request authorizing you to make the request on their behalf.&nbsp; The written permission must state your full legal name, the full legal name of the individual who is the subject of the request, and needs to be clear about the permission granted.&nbsp; Alternatively, you may submit a copy of a power of attorney under Probate Code sections 4000-4465. In either case, please also indicate in your email the nature of your request. The consumer’s identity, in addition to your own, will need to be independently verified in order for us to be able to fulfill your request.&nbsp; We may also ask the consumer to directly confirm with us that they provided you permission to submit a request. Please keep in mind that if we do not receive adequate proof that you are authorized to act on the consumer’s behalf, we may deny the request.</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.533121s;"><strong>How to Make Request to Know or Request to Delete</strong></p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.535032s;">If you are a California resident and would like to request information about the Personal Information we have collected about you in the prior 12 months or to request that we delete your information, please contact us at <a href="mailto:legal@madisonwellsmedia.com">legal@madisonwellsmedia.com</a>.</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.536943s;"><strong>Verifying Requests</strong></p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.538854s;">Please provide your first and last name, email address you have used to interact with MWM, mailing address, and telephone number, which we will use to verify your request. We may ask for additional information as needed to fully verify you or your request.</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.540764s;">If we are unable to verify that the individual submitting the request is the same individual about whom we have collected information (or someone authorized by that individual to act on their behalf), we will not be able to process the request.</p><h3 style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.542675s;" class="preSlide">Other Important Information</h3><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.544586s;"><strong>Request to Know</strong></p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.546497s;">In order to have us provide specific pieces of information, we will require a signed declaration under penalty of perjury that you are the consumer whose Personal Information is the subject of the request. &nbsp;</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.548408s;"><strong>Request to Delete</strong></p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.550318s;">To ensure that we do not delete your personal information in response to a fraudulent request, once you submit the request, we will follow up to confirm that you want your information to be deleted.&nbsp;</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.552229s;"><strong><em>THE SALE OF PERSONAL INFORMATION</em> </strong>MWM does not believe that it engages in sales of personal information as defined by the CCPA.<strong> </strong>Accordingly, MWM does not knowingly sell Personal Information of minors younger than 16 years of age.</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.55414s;"><strong><em>Right to Non-Discrimination for the Exercise of a Consumer’s Privacy Rights</em></strong></p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.556051s;">California consumers have the right to not receive discriminatory treatment for exercising CCPA rights.&nbsp; We will not discriminate against you for exercising your CCPA rights.&nbsp;</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.557962s;"><strong>Contact for More Information&nbsp;</strong></p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.559873s;">You can contact us for more information at <a href="mailto:legal@madisonwellsmedia.com">legal@madisonwellsmedia.com</a> or write to us at the following mailing address: CA Privacy Rights, Madison Wells Media, LLC, Attn: Business and Legal Affairs, 1999 Avenue of the Stars, Suite 1500 Los Angeles, CA 90067.<strong>&nbsp;</strong></p>
</div>



</div></div><div class="sqs-block code-block sqs-block-code" data-block-type="23" id="block-yui_3_17_2_1_1593042354342_138050"><div class="sqs-block-content"><p id="ca-privacy-rights" class="preFade" style="transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.561783s;"><a id="back-to-top" href="#top">Back to Top ⇡</a></p></div></div><div class="sqs-block html-block sqs-block-html" data-block-type="2" id="block-yui_3_17_2_1_1593042354342_138117"><div class="sqs-block-content">

<div class="sqs-html-content">
  <ol data-rte-list="default"><li><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.563694s;"><strong>Your California Privacy Rights</strong></p></li></ol><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.565605s;">Pursuant to California Civil Code Section 1798.83, residents of the State of California have the right to request from companies conducting business in California certain information relating to third parties to which the company has disclosed certain categories of personal information during the preceding year for the third parties' direct marketing purposes. Alternatively, the law provides that a company may comply, as MWM does, by disclosing in its privacy policy that it provides consumers choice (opt-out or opt-in) regarding sharing personal information with third parties for those third parties’ direct marketing purposes, and information on how to exercise that choice.&nbsp; As stated above in this Privacy Policy, MWM provides you choice prior to sharing your personal information with third parties for their direct marketing purposes. If you do not opt-in or if you choose to opt-out at the time MWM offers that choice, MWM does not share your information with that identified third party for its direct marketing purposes.</p><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.567516s;">If you are a California resident and have questions about our practices with respect to sharing information with third parties for their direct marketing purposes and your ability to exercise choice, please send your request via email to <a href="mailto:legal@madisonwellsmedia.com">legal@madisonwellsmedia.com</a> or write to us at the following mailing address: CA Privacy Rights, Madison Wells Media, LLC, Attn: Business and Legal Affairs, 1999 Avenue of the Stars, Suite 1500 Los Angeles, CA 90067. You must put the statement “Your California Privacy Rights” in the subject field of your email or include it in your writing if you choose to write to us at the designated mailing address. You must include your name, street address, city, state, and zip code. We are not responsible for notices that are not labeled or sent properly, or do not have complete information.</p>
</div>



</div></div><div class="sqs-block code-block sqs-block-code" data-block-type="23" id="block-yui_3_17_2_1_1593029317331_99108"><div class="sqs-block-content"><p id="nv-resident-notice" class="preFade" style="transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.569427s;"><a id="back-to-top" href="#top">Back to Top ⇡</a></p></div></div><div class="sqs-block html-block sqs-block-html" data-block-type="2" id="block-yui_3_17_2_1_1593029317331_99174"><div class="sqs-block-content">

<div class="sqs-html-content">
  <h3 style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.571338s;" class="preSlide">NOTICE TO NEVADA RESIDENTS&nbsp;</h3><p class="preFade" style="white-space: pre-wrap; transition-timing-function: ease; transition-duration: 0.6s; transition-delay: 0.573248s;">Pursuant to Nevada law, consumers in Nevada have the right to opt-out of the sale of certain personally identifiable information we have collected about you through our Services.&nbsp; Please note that MWM does not currently sell your covered information as those terms are defined under applicable Nevada law. However, you may still submit an opt-out of future sales and we will honor that request as required by Nevada law, if MWM were to engage in such a sale in the future. If you are a Nevada resident and would like to opt-out of future sales of your information, you must submit your request to <a href="mailto:legal@madisonwellsmedia.com">legal@madisonwellsmedia.com</a>. Your request must include “Nevada Opt-Out” in the subject line and the email should include your full name, street address, city, state, and zip code. Please contact us from the email address you have used to interact with us, or else provide us with that email address so that we can contact you if needed regarding this request. If you previously provided a phone number to us, including it will assist us in making sure we identify you as someone who wants to proactively opt-out and processing your request. We are not responsible for requests that do not come through the designated request mechanism or do not contain sufficient information to allow us to process your request. You may also be required to take reasonable steps as we determine from time to time in order to verify your identity and/or the authenticity of the request. We<em> </em>will respond to your request within sixty (60) days either confirming that your request has been processed or indicating that we need an additional thirty (30) days to complete the request.</p>
</div>
